## Products

- [Women's Tee — "God Is WITHIN" Floral Psalm 46:5 Faith Tee](https://faithbloom.co/products/god-is-within-her-christian-tee): This tee carries a quiet, confident voice. Bold letters spelling WITHIN are filled with a garden of roses and greenery, framed so the floral detail reads as both delicate and unapologetically strong. Above, “GOD IS” sits in restrained small caps; beneath, a soft-script “she will not fall” settles like a whispered promise, with Psalm 46:5 tucked subtly below. Wear it to Bible study, church, or on mornings when you need a gentle reminder that faith and feminine strength can live together — a shirt that speaks of rooted hope rather than shouting for attention.Product features- Side seams for improved shape retention and structure- Elastic ribbed knit collar with seam to maintain neckline- Lightweight 100% Airlume combed and ringspun cotton (color variations may apply)- Slim fit with longer body length; runs smaller than usual- Tear-away label and shoulder tape for comfort and long-term stabilityCare instructions- Machine wash: warm (max 40C or 105F)- Non-chlorine: bleach as needed- Tumble dry: low heat- Iron, steam or dry: medium heat- Do not dryclean

The bold, oversized “WALK” stacked over a distressed “Faith” inside a grunge circle reads confidently from across a room—quiet testimony without saying a word. It slips easily into youth nights, casual church gatherings, weekend outreach, or everyday streetwear. Short, sturdy seams and a ribbed collar keep it looking sharp after washes. Wear it with a worn denim jacket for sermon nights or with joggers on outreach runs; it’s the shirt that carries the message while you live it out.Product features- Durable double-needle stitching on sleeves and hem for long-lasting wear- Ribbed collar that stretches on and returns to shape for a clean fit- Medium-weight fabric (6.0 oz/yd²) with mostly 100% cotton options- Twill neck and shoulder tape to prevent stretching and stabilize seams- Tear-away label and DTF inner neck print for comfortable, low-profile wearCare instructions- Machine wash: cold (max 30C or 90F)- Do not bleach- Tumble dry: low heat- Iron, steam or dry: low heat- Do not dryclean

This oversized boxy tee wears a sunset — bands of orange, gold, and red melting into a deep green tree that subtly forms a cross. The distressed lettering, arched with “HE RESTORES MY SOUL” and Psalm 23:3 beneath, feels like a beloved message passed down through seasons. It settles easily over shoulders, drapes with a relaxed silhouette, and brings a quiet, steady reassurance to mornings with coffee, porch chats, or slow drives back home. - [Eucharist 'Real Power' Tee — Radiant Host & Chalice Catholic T-Shirt](https://faithbloom.co/products/sacred-heart-chalice-eucharist-t-shirt): This tee puts faith on display with quiet strength. A distressed metallic-gold arch reading “EUCHARIST” crowns a radiant Host set in a golden chalice. From the Host, a glowing cross rises through red flames, framed by subtle rays—a visual statement of Christ’s real presence and power. The phrase “REAL POWER” grounds the design below, pairing streetwear boldness with reverent symbolism. The slightly oversized, medium-weight cotton gives a vintage, broken-in feel that wears comfortably through weekday Mass, evening adoration, or a faith-centered meet-up. Wear it with prayerful confidence—this shirt reads like a declaration, not a slogan.Product features- Tubular knit (no side seams) for a cleaner drape and reduced fabric waste- Ribbed collar and shoulder tape for durability and shape retention- Medium-weight, environmentally-minded cotton with a vintage, thicker hand (6.0 oz/yd²)- Runs slightly large for extra comfort and easy layering- Tear-away label and Oeko-Tex/ethical cotton certifications for safer, longer-lasting wearCare instructions- Machine wash: cold (max 30C or 90F)- Non-chlorine: bleach as needed- Do not tumble dry- Do not iron- Do not dryclean

It feels like a whispered prayer you can wear — light and breathable, with a familiar vintage edge from the contrasting collar and sleeve bands. Slip it on for long summer evenings at the parish picnic, slow walks to Eucharistic adoration, or when you want a subtle, contemporary expression of faith that reads calm and thoughtful rather than loud. - [Eat, Pray, Don’t Sin (Too Much!) Catholic Tee — Spirit of the Vine Stained-Glass Wine T-Shirt](https://faithbloom.co/products/eat-pray-dont-mess-up-much-tee): This midweight cotton tee brings a little wicked humor to Sunday best. The design feels like a stained-glass chapel come alive: a glowing cross crowns a rich bottle labeled “Spirit of the Vine,” a full glass ready to pour, and clusters of grapes and wheat anchoring the scene. Warm reds, golds, and greens give the artwork a cozy, church-window glow, while bold black lettering with a white outline makes the cheeky banner—“Eat, Pray, Don’t Sin (Too Much!)”—pop on darker shirts. It sits comfortably against the skin, holds its shape through wear, and reads like an inside joke shared among friends who love faith, fellowship, and a good toast.Product features- 100% cotton solid colors; blends for heather/antique shades- Medium-weight fabric (5.3 oz/yd²) for structure and comfort- Double-needle hems for added durability- Side seams and neck/shoulder tape to retain shape- Semi-fitted cut with tear-away label for comfortCare instructions- Machine wash: cold (max 30C or 90F)- Do not bleach- Tumble dry: low heat- Iron, steam or dry: low heat- Do not dryclean

It sits comfortably in everyday life: layered under a flannel for errands, worn solo at small group meetups, or thrown on after Sunday service. The shirt feels modern and intentional — simple lines, strong message, and easy-to-wear fabric that moves with you. Above, vintage block type reads SOFT HEART · SOLID ROCK, with Ezekiel 36:26 and Matthew 7:24–25 beneath. It’s more than art; it’s a quiet declaration of faith: a tender heart renewed by God and a life anchored on the firm truth of Scripture. The shirt drapes easily, moves with you, and becomes a wearable reminder in everyday moments — worship nights, small-group meetups, or simply walking through your neighborhood. - [Faith Over Fear T-Shirt — Inspirational Christian Tee](https://faithbloom.co/products/faith-over-fear-t-shirt-inspirational-christian-tee): Soft, breathable cotton tee with a quiet, confident message: FAITH over FEAR printed across the chest. The lightweight Bella Canvas fabric feels gentle against skin and layers easily under jackets or over long sleeves. Clean, minimalist typography keeps the focus on the message, while quality finishing—side seams, ribbed collar, shoulder tape, and a tear-away label—means this shirt keeps its shape and stays comfortable through repeated wear. Wear it to church gatherings, community meetups, or slower weekend mornings when you want clothing that reflects steady conviction rather than loud slogans.Product features- 100% Airlume combed and ring-spun cotton (lightweight 4.2 oz) for breathable comfort- Side seams and shoulder tape provide structure and shape retention- Ribbed knit collar with seam and tear-away label for comfort and durability- High-detail sleeve and neck prints produced with DTF/DTG techniques for crisp, vibrant designs- REACH certified; sourced blank from Honduras; ethically manufactured processesCare instructions- Machine wash: cold (max 30C or 90F)- Non-chlorine: bleach as needed- Tumble dry: low heat- Iron, steam or dry: medium heat- Do not drycleanEU representative: HONSON VENTURES LIMITED, gpsr@honsonventures.com, 3, Gnaftis House flat 102, Limassol, Mesa Geitonia, 4003, CY Product information: Bella+Canvas 3001, 2 year warranty in EU and Northern Ireland as per Directive 1999/44/EC Warnings, Hazard: For adults, Blank product sourced from Honduras Care instructions: Machine wash: cold (max 30C or 90F), Non-chlorine: bleach as needed, Tumble dry: low heat, Iron, steam or dry: medium heat, Do not dryclean

It feels like a late-night walk along the shore — salt air, steady conviction, and the comfort of something that won’t move when emotions rise.
